In early training, the critic is inaccurate, and updating the actor from a bad critic pushes the policy in the wrong direction. Delaying actor updates gives the critics more time to converge on each policy before the policy is updated. Fewer, more reliable actor updates outperform frequent, noisy ones."]}]
